the universal type identity system used across all sub-projects\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go` — implements Scheme: the runtime registry mapping GVKs to Go reflect.Types; core of all type registration and conversion\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go` — defines the Object, Encoder, Decoder, and GroupVersioner interfaces; the foundational contracts for all serialization\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go` — defines TypeMeta (Kind + APIVersion) and ObjectMeta (name, namespace, labels, resourceVersion, etc.); embedded in every Kubernetes object\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go` — defines Unstructured: a map[string]interface{} wrapper that implements runtime.Object, metav1.Object, and schema.ObjectKind; the representation for all custom resources at runtime\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver (CRD Type Definitions + Server-Side Lifecycle)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go` — internal hub types for CustomResourceDefinition (CustomResourceDefinitionSpec, CustomResourceDefinitionNames, CustomResourceValidation, etc.); used internally by the server and never serialized\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` — registers internal hub types to the Scheme under GroupVersion `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go` — external v1 types (CustomResourceDefinitionSpec with JSON/protobuf tags); this is the wire-format representation persisted to etcd and served over the API\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/register.go` — registers v1 external types to the Scheme under GroupVersion `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`; also registers defaulting functions via SchemeBuilder\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/install/install.go` — installs all CRD API versions (internal, v1beta1, v1) into a Scheme at once; called during server startup\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` — validates CRD objects: name format, OpenAPI schema structure, CEL expression cost budgets, version consistency; called by the create/update strategy\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` — implements the REST storage for CRD objects themselves (not CRs) backed by the generic etcd registry; uses the internal hub type in NewFunc/NewListFunc\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` — implements storage for actual custom resource instances; NewFunc returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` with the GVK pre-set; uses genericregistry.Store for full etcd CRUD\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` — server bootstrap: creates the Scheme, registers the CRD REST endpoint, instantiates the typed clientset and informer factory, then registers the crdHandler as a dynamic HTTP filter\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` — the central HTTP dispatch layer (crdHandler); watches the CRD informer for changes, dynamically creates/destroys per-GVR storage and request scopes; routes all `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>` traffic to the appropriate `customresource.CustomResourceStorage`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go` — generated typed clientset for managing CRD objects; exposes `ApiextensionsV1()` returning a client for CRUD on `CustomResourceDefinition` resources\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/informers/externalversions/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` — generated SharedIndexInformer for CRD objects; uses a ListWatch backed by the typed clientset; the crdHandler holds a reference to this informer's lister\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` — generated lister backed by a cache.Indexer; provides `List(labels.Selector)` and `Get(name)` returning `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition`\n\n### client-go (Generic + Dynamic Client-Side Access)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` — DynamicClient: a GVR-parameterized REST client that serializes/deserializes all objects as `*unstructured.Unstructured`; uses `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).Create/Get/List/Watch/...`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` — DynamicSharedInformerFactory: creates SharedIndexInformers keyed by GVR; each informer uses `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` as the object type; bridges dynamic client with the cache layer\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` — dynamicLister: a GVR-aware lister over a cache.Indexer returning `*unstructured.Unstructured`; used by dynamic informers to provide read access to the local cache\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/factory.go` — SharedInformerFactory: the standard typed informer factory for core/built-in API groups; not used for CRs directly but defines the SharedIndexInformer pattern shared by the dynamic and typed paths\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/interface.go` — Interface definition for DynamicClient; defined in terms of GVR and Unstructured\n\n### api (Standard Group Registration Reference)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/` — contains versioned Go structs for built-in API groups (core, apps, batch, etc.); illustrates the same external-type + register.go pattern that apiextensions-apiserver follows, and whose ObjectMeta/TypeMeta originate from apimachinery\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Foundation (apimachinery)**: `schema.GroupVersionKind` / `schema.GroupVersionResource` → `runtime.Scheme` (GVK↔reflect.Type registry) → `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta` → `unstructured.Unstructured` (dynamic object representation)\n\n2. **Type Definitions (apiextensions-apiserver)**:\n   - Internal hub types (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`) import `metav1` for ObjectMeta; registered as `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n   - External v1 types (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`) import `metav1` + `runtime` for JSON/protobuf serialization; registered as `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`\n   - `install.Install(scheme)` registers both in one call, establishing the version conversion chain\n\n3. **Server-Side: Validation → Storage → HTTP Handler**:\n   - `validation/validation.go` validates new/updated CRD objects (structural schema, CEL, naming rules) using internal hub types\n   - `registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` stores the CRD object itself in etcd via `genericregistry.Store`; uses `apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition` (internal) in NewFunc\n   - Upon a new/updated CRD being stored, the `crdHandler` receives an event from the CRD informer, calls `getOrCreateServingInfoFor()` which builds a new `customresource.CustomResourceStorage` (backed by etcd, keyed to the CRD's GVR), and registers request scopes for that GVR\n   - `registry/customresource/etcd.go` is the actual per-GVR storage; `NewFunc` returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` — proving that the server stores custom resources as Unstructured objects in etcd\n   - `apiserver/customresource_handler.go` dynamically routes HTTP requests to the appropriate storage/scope based on CRD lister lookups (crdInfo.storages map)\n\n4. **Client-Side: Typed Client → Informer → Lister → Dynamic Client**:\n   - `client/clientset/clientset.go` (apiextensions-apiserver) — typed CRUD for the CRD *definition* resource; used by the server's own crdHandler and by controllers\n   - `client/informers/.../customresourcedefinition.go` — CRD informer backed by the typed clientset; the crdHandler holds a reference to watch for CRD additions/deletions\n   - `client/listers/.../customresourcedefinition.go` — cache-backed lister used inside crdHandler to look up CRDs during request dispatch\n   - `client-go/dynamic/simple.go` (DynamicClient) — for accessing *instances* of custom resources; uses GVR + Unstructured; no Go struct needed for the CR type\n   - `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` — watches CR instances over the DynamicClient using `&unstructured.Unstructured{}`; caches them in a SharedIndexInformer\n   - `client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` — reads from the dynamic informer's Indexer, returning `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery\n  schema.GVK / schema.GVR\n  runtime.Scheme\n  metav1.TypeMeta, metav1.ObjectMeta\n  unstructured.Unstructured\n       ↓ imported by all three\napiextensions-apiserver\n  Internal hub types  ←→  External v1 types\n  validation (CEL, OpenAPI)\n  etcd storage (CRD definition + CR instances)\n  crdHandler (dynamic HTTP routing)\n  typed clientset / informer / lister (for CRD definitions)\n       ↓ server writes, clients read\nclient-go\n  DynamicClient (GVR + Unstructured)\n  DynamicSharedInformerFactory (GVR-keyed informers)\n  dynamicLister (cache.Indexer → Unstructured)\n       ↑ both depend on apimachinery\nk8s.io/api\n  Built-in group types (same pattern: external versioned types + register.go)\n  ObjectMeta/TypeMeta come from apimachinery\n```\n\n### How CRD Types Bridge the Four Sub-Projects\n\nThe CRD lifecycle starts in **apimachinery**: every type in every sub-project is identified by a `schema.GroupVersionKind` and stored/retrieved via a `runtime.Scheme`. TypeMeta and ObjectMeta — defined in `apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1` — are embedded by every Kubernetes object, including `CustomResourceDefinition` itself.\n\nIn **apiextensions-apiserver**, the CRD type is defined twice: an internal hub struct (no JSON tags, used for in-process manipulation) and an external v1 struct (with JSON/protobuf tags, used for serialization). The `install` package wires both into the server's Scheme via `AddToScheme`. When a user POSTs a CRD, the server decodes the JSON into the external v1 type, converts it to the internal type for validation, runs validation, converts back to v1, and writes it to etcd. The `crdHandler` maintains an informer cache of CRD definitions; when a new CRD appears or changes, it dynamically registers or tears down the corresponding HTTP handler and etcd storage for that GVR.\n\nIn **k8s.io/api**, the same external-type + register.go pattern is used for built-in API groups (Pods, Deployments, etc.), demonstrating that the pattern is consistent across the monorepo. CRDs allow user-defined groups to follow the same pattern without needing compiled Go structs.\n\n### The Role of Scheme and GVK in Type Registration\n\n`runtime.Scheme` is the central registry that maps GVKs to Go reflect.Types. When `install.Install(scheme)` is called at server startup, it registers:\n- `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal` → `apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition` (Go internal type)\n- `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1` → `v1.CustomResourceDefinition` (Go external type)\n- Conversion functions between the two\n\nAt CR request time, the crdHandler dynamically creates a new minimal Scheme containing only the specific GVK for the requested custom resource version. The `NewFunc` in the customresource storage returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` pre-populated with that GVK — no static Go type is needed. The codec factory for that custom Scheme then uses the Unstructured type for all serialization.\n\n### How Unstructured Enables Dynamic Custom Resource Access\n\n`unstructured.Unstructured` (defined in `apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured`) is a `map[string]interface{}` that implements `runtime.Object`, `metav1.Object`, and `schema.ObjectKind`. This allows it to:\n1. Be stored in etcd by the `genericregistry.Store` (which requires runtime.Object)\n2. Have its TypeMeta/ObjectMeta accessed by the API machinery (which requires metav1.Object)\n3. Be serialized/deserialized as JSON without schema-specific Go structs\n\nThe **DynamicClient** (`client-go/dynamic/simple.go`) uses Unstructured exclusively: it encodes requests and decodes responses via `unstructured.UnstructuredJSONScheme`. This means any custom resource — regardless of its OpenAPI schema or group — can be accessed, watched, and cached without any code generation or compiled type knowledge.\n\nThe **DynamicSharedInformerFactory** (`client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go`) creates a `cache.SharedIndexInformer` with `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` as the example object type. The ListWatch functions call `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).List/Watch`, returning Unstructured objects that are stored in the informer's Indexer. The **dynamicLister** then reads from that Indexer, returning `[]*unstructured.Unstructured`.\n\n### The Checkpoint Between Server-Side Storage and Client-Side Informer Caching\n\nThe boundary between server-side and client-side is the Kubernetes API HTTP layer:\n\n1. **Server side**: the `crdHandler` receives an HTTP request for `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>`, looks up the CRD via the lister, finds the corresponding `customresource.CustomResourceStorage`, and delegates to the generic REST handler (which reads/writes etcd). For watch requests, it streams `WatchEvent` objects.\n\n2. **Client side**: the DynamicClient or typed clientset opens an HTTP watch stream to that same endpoint. The `cache.SharedIndexInformer`'s reflector continuously consumes the watch stream, calling `Add`/`Update`/`Delete` on the local thread-safe store (Indexer). The lister then reads from this Indexer.\n\nThe key mechanism enabling this is that the server supports `?watch=true` on any CRD endpoint (because genericregistry.Store implements `Watch()`), and the informer's ListWatch uses this. The informer re-lists periodically and on reconnect to resync. This means the client-side cache is eventually consistent with etcd, with the CRD informer in the crdHandler used server-side and the DynamicSharedInformerFactory used client-side — but both ultimately consume the same HTTP watch protocol.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nA CRD flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem in four stages: (1) apimachinery provides the foundational GVK/GVR identity types, Scheme registry, TypeMeta/ObjectMeta, and Unstructured representation that all sub-projects depend on; (2) apiextensions-apiserver defines the CRD type in both internal hub and external v1 forms, validates it via CEL/OpenAPI rules, persists CRD definitions and CR instances to etcd using genericregistry.Store (with CRs stored as Unstructured), and dynamically routes HTTP traffic through the crdHandler which reacts to CRD informer events; (3) the typed clientset/informer/lister (generated in apiextensions-apiserver) manage CRD *definitions*, while the DynamicClient/DynamicSharedInformerFactory/dynamicLister (in client-go) access CRD *instances* as Unstructured objects without requiring any compiled Go structs; (4) k8s.io/api demonstrates the same external-type + register.go pattern for built-in groups, confirming that CRDs are a first-class extension of a uniform type registration and serving architecture.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":108,"cache_read_input_tokens":51512,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":108,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":21,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"229d1523-fede-4242-a942-c6630b74011d","uuid":"f3ca1196-9dc0-4103-b230-89d12e4ff099"}

the universal type identity system used across all sub-projects\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go` — implements Scheme: the runtime registry mapping GVKs to Go reflect.Types; core of all type registration and conversion\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go` — defines the Object, Encoder, Decoder, and GroupVersioner interfaces; the foundational contracts for all serialization\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go` — defines TypeMeta (Kind + APIVersion) and ObjectMeta (name, namespace, labels, resourceVersion, etc.); embedded in every Kubernetes object\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go` — defines Unstructured: a map[string]interface{} wrapper that implements runtime.Object, metav1.Object, and schema.ObjectKind; the representation for all custom resources at runtime\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver (CRD Type Definitions + Server-Side Lifecycle)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go` — internal hub types for CustomResourceDefinition (CustomResourceDefinitionSpec, CustomResourceDefinitionNames, CustomResourceValidation, etc.); used internally by the server and never serialized\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` — registers internal hub types to the Scheme under GroupVersion `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go` — external v1 types (CustomResourceDefinitionSpec with JSON/protobuf tags); this is the wire-format representation persisted to etcd and served over the API\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/register.go` — registers v1 external types to the Scheme under GroupVersion `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`; also registers defaulting functions via SchemeBuilder\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/install/install.go` — installs all CRD API versions (internal, v1beta1, v1) into a Scheme at once; called during server startup\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` — validates CRD objects: name format, OpenAPI schema structure, CEL expression cost budgets, version consistency; called by the create/update strategy\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` — implements the REST storage for CRD objects themselves (not CRs) backed by the generic etcd registry; uses the internal hub type in NewFunc/NewListFunc\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` — implements storage for actual custom resource instances; NewFunc returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` with the GVK pre-set; uses genericregistry.Store for full etcd CRUD\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` — server bootstrap: creates the Scheme, registers the CRD REST endpoint, instantiates the typed clientset and informer factory, then registers the crdHandler as a dynamic HTTP filter\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` — the central HTTP dispatch layer (crdHandler); watches the CRD informer for changes, dynamically creates/destroys per-GVR storage and request scopes; routes all `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>` traffic to the appropriate `customresource.CustomResourceStorage`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go` — generated typed clientset for managing CRD objects; exposes `ApiextensionsV1()` returning a client for CRUD on `CustomResourceDefinition` resources\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/informers/externalversions/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` — generated SharedIndexInformer for CRD objects; uses a ListWatch backed by the typed clientset; the crdHandler holds a reference to this informer's lister\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` — generated lister backed by a cache.Indexer; provides `List(labels.Selector)` and `Get(name)` returning `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition`\n\n### client-go (Generic + Dynamic Client-Side Access)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` — DynamicClient: a GVR-parameterized REST client that serializes/deserializes all objects as `*unstructured.Unstructured`; uses `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).Create/Get/List/Watch/...`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` — DynamicSharedInformerFactory: creates SharedIndexInformers keyed by GVR; each informer uses `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` as the object type; bridges dynamic client with the cache layer\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` — dynamicLister: a GVR-aware lister over a cache.Indexer returning `*unstructured.Unstructured`; used by dynamic informers to provide read access to the local cache\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/factory.go` — SharedInformerFactory: the standard typed informer factory for core/built-in API groups; not used for CRs directly but defines the SharedIndexInformer pattern shared by the dynamic and typed paths\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/interface.go` — Interface definition for DynamicClient; defined in terms of GVR and Unstructured\n\n### api (Standard Group Registration Reference)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/` — contains versioned Go structs for built-in API groups (core, apps, batch, etc.); illustrates the same external-type + register.go pattern that apiextensions-apiserver follows, and whose ObjectMeta/TypeMeta originate from apimachinery\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Foundation (apimachinery)**: `schema.GroupVersionKind` / `schema.GroupVersionResource` → `runtime.Scheme` (GVK↔reflect.Type registry) → `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta` → `unstructured.Unstructured` (dynamic object representation)\n\n2. **Type Definitions (apiextensions-apiserver)**:\n   - Internal hub types (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`) import `metav1` for ObjectMeta; registered as `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n   - External v1 types (`pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`) import `metav1` + `runtime` for JSON/protobuf serialization; registered as `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`\n   - `install.Install(scheme)` registers both in one call, establishing the version conversion chain\n\n3. **Server-Side: Validation → Storage → HTTP Handler**:\n   - `validation/validation.go` validates new/updated CRD objects (structural schema, CEL, naming rules) using internal hub types\n   - `registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` stores the CRD object itself in etcd via `genericregistry.Store`; uses `apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition` (internal) in NewFunc\n   - Upon a new/updated CRD being stored, the `crdHandler` receives an event from the CRD informer, calls `getOrCreateServingInfoFor()` which builds a new `customresource.CustomResourceStorage` (backed by etcd, keyed to the CRD's GVR), and registers request scopes for that GVR\n   - `registry/customresource/etcd.go` is the actual per-GVR storage; `NewFunc` returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` — proving that the server stores custom resources as Unstructured objects in etcd\n   - `apiserver/customresource_handler.go` dynamically routes HTTP requests to the appropriate storage/scope based on CRD lister lookups (crdInfo.storages map)\n\n4. **Client-Side: Typed Client → Informer → Lister → Dynamic Client**:\n   - `client/clientset/clientset.go` (apiextensions-apiserver) — typed CRUD for the CRD *definition* resource; used by the server's own crdHandler and by controllers\n   - `client/informers/.../customresourcedefinition.go` — CRD informer backed by the typed clientset; the crdHandler holds a reference to watch for CRD additions/deletions\n   - `client/listers/.../customresourcedefinition.go` — cache-backed lister used inside crdHandler to look up CRDs during request dispatch\n   - `client-go/dynamic/simple.go` (DynamicClient) — for accessing *instances* of custom resources; uses GVR + Unstructured; no Go struct needed for the CR type\n   - `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` — watches CR instances over the DynamicClient using `&unstructured.Unstructured{}`; caches them in a SharedIndexInformer\n   - `client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` — reads from the dynamic informer's Indexer, returning `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery\n  schema.GVK / schema.GVR\n  runtime.Scheme\n  metav1.TypeMeta, metav1.ObjectMeta\n  unstructured.Unstructured\n       ↓ imported by all three\napiextensions-apiserver\n  Internal hub types  ←→  External v1 types\n  validation (CEL, OpenAPI)\n  etcd storage (CRD definition + CR instances)\n  crdHandler (dynamic HTTP routing)\n  typed clientset / informer / lister (for CRD definitions)\n       ↓ server writes, clients read\nclient-go\n  DynamicClient (GVR + Unstructured)\n  DynamicSharedInformerFactory (GVR-keyed informers)\n  dynamicLister (cache.Indexer → Unstructured)\n       ↑ both depend on apimachinery\nk8s.io/api\n  Built-in group types (same pattern: external versioned types + register.go)\n  ObjectMeta/TypeMeta come from apimachinery\n```\n\n### How CRD Types Bridge the Four Sub-Projects\n\nThe CRD lifecycle starts in **apimachinery**: every type in every sub-project is identified by a `schema.GroupVersionKind` and stored/retrieved via a `runtime.Scheme`.
